A win or a loss against AlphaStar will affect your MMR as normal.</n></n>Thank you to everyone who has helped our work with DeepMind so far, and to all those who continue to support us as we push the boundaries of what’s possible in StarCraft! /// We’re excited to announce that experimental versions of DeepMind’s StarCraft II agent, AlphaStar, will soon play a small number of games on the competitive ladder as part of ongoing scientific research into artificial intelligence.</n></n>If you would like the chance to help DeepMind with its research by matching against AlphaStar, you can <s val="Versus_AgentsOnLadderOptIn_SectionTextHighlight">opt-in</s> by clicking the button below. UI/UserProfileLadderDivisionFrame/GrandmasterInfo=宗师联赛是一级开放了有限席位的特殊联赛，它为各个地区顶尖的《星际争霸II》选手提供了进行切磋的竞技舞台。<n/><n/>晋升宗师联赛的资格将在每个新赛季开始一周后进行评定。经过新赛季第一周的角逐后，符合晋级条件的选手必须再赛一场才能成功晋升。宗师联赛排名是逐日计算的，因此低于MMR分割线的玩家将从宗师联赛中降级，为其他超过MMR水准线的玩家腾出席位。<n/><n/>在宗师联赛中获得席位的玩家将被分进一个“争夺者名单”，在那里他们可以更清楚地查看玩家们争取下一次宗师联赛晋级资格的对战情况。降级的玩家会被“争夺者名单”给予一个窗口期，给他们一次在当天排名结算之前赢回席位的最后机会。<n/><n/>要想保住宗师联赛席位，每3周至少要打30场比赛。奖励池在宗师联赛中不会累积。如果一名玩家不够活跃，他将会自动降级，其席位将会被一位高活跃度的新玩家所取代。<n/><n/>祝贺所有成功晋升宗师联赛的玩家，祝大家好运！ /// The Grandmaster League is an exclusive league with limited open slots where the top StarCraft II players in each region can compete against each other to test their mettle.<n/><n/>Qualification is determined after the first week in a new season. After the first week, candidates must play one more match in order to receive their promotion. Grandmaster rankings are calculated daily, thus players below the MMR cutoff will be demoted from Grandmaster to make room for those who are above the required MMR threshold.<n/><n/>Players positioned for a spot in Grandmaster will be placed into a Contender List, where they can more easily view the players battling for a coveted slot in the next Grandmaster promotion. Demoted players will have a window of time in the Contender List to earn their spot back before the rankings are calculated for that day.<n/><n/>In order to retain a spot in Grandmaster, a minimum of 30 games every 3 weeks must be played. Bonus pool is not accumulated in Grandmaster. If a player is inactive, they will be automatically demoted and a more active combatant will fill the empty slot.<n/><n/>Congratulations to all those qualified in the Grandmaster League and good luck!
